Fluid Mech.</i>, <b>23</b> (4): 801–819, <a href="/wiki/Bibcode" title="Bibcode">Bibcode</a>:<a class="external text" href="http://adsabs.harvard.edu/abs/1965JFM....23..801W" rel="nofollow">1965JFM....23..801W</a>, <a href="/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" title="Digital object identifier">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="//doi.org/10.1017%2Fs0022112065001702" rel="nofollow">10.1017/s0022112065001702</a></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=J.+Fluid+Mech.&amp;rft.atitle=Report+on+the+first+European+Mechanics+Colloquium%2C+on+the+Coanda+effect&amp;rft.volume=23&amp;rft.issue=4&amp;rft.pages=801-819&amp;rft.date=1965&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1017%2Fs0022112065001702&amp;rft_id=info%3Abibcode%2F1965JFM....23..801W&amp;rft.aulast=Wille&amp;rft.aufirst=R.&amp;rft.au=Fernholz%2C+H.&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALift+%28force%29"></span><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/></li>
<li><cite class="citation" id="CITEREFWilliamsonGovardhan2004">Williamson, C. H. K.; Govardhan, R (2004), "Vortex-induced vibrations", <i>Annual Review of Fluid Mechanics</i>, <b>36</b>: 413–455, <a href="/wiki/Bibcode" title="Bibcode">Bibcode</a>:<a class="external text" href="http://adsabs.harvard.edu/abs/2004AnRFM..36..413W" rel="nofollow">2004AnRFM..36..413W</a>, <a href="/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" title="Digital object identifier">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="//doi.org/10.1146%2Fannurev.fluid.36.050802.122128" rel="nofollow">10.1146/annurev.fluid.36.050802.122128</a></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Annual+Review+of+Fluid+Mechanics&amp;rft.atitle=Vortex-induced+vibrations&amp;rft.volume=36&amp;rft.pages=413-455&amp;rft.date=2004&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1146%2Fannurev.fluid.36.050802.122128&amp;rft_id=info%3Abibcode%2F2004AnRFM..36..413W&amp;rft.aulast=Williamson&amp;rft.aufirst=C.+H.+K.&amp;rft.au=Govardhan%2C+R&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALift+%28force%29"></span><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/></li>
<li><cite class="citation" id="CITEREFZdravkovich2003">Zdravkovich, M. M. (2003), <i>Flow around circular cylinders 2</i>, Oxford University Press, pp. 850–855, <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-19-856561-5" title="Special:BookSources/0-19-856561-5">0-19-856561-5</a></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Flow+around+circular+cylinders+2&amp;rft.pages=850-855&amp;rft.pub=Oxford+University+Press&amp;rft.date=2003&amp;rft.isbn=0-19-856561-5&amp;rft.aulast=Zdravkovich&amp;rft.aufirst=M.+M.&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALift+%28force%29"></span><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Further_reading">Further reading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Lift_(force)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Further reading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r853264625">.mw-parser-output .refbegin{font-size:90%;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul{list-style-type:none;margin-left:0}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul>li,.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>dl>dd{margin-left:0;padding-left:3.2em;text-indent:-3.2em;list-style:none}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-100{font-size:100%}</style><div class="refbegin columns references-column-count references-column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
<ul><li><i>Introduction to Flight</i>, John D. Anderson, Jr., McGraw-Hill, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-07-299071-6" title="Special:BookSources/0-07-299071-6">0-07-299071-6</a> – Dr. Anderson is Curator of Aerodynamics at the Smithsonian Institution's National Air &amp; Space Museum and Professor Emeritus at the University of Maryland.</li>
<li><i>Understanding Flight</i>, by David Anderson and Scott Eberhardt, McGraw-Hill, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-07-136377-7" title="Special:BookSources/0-07-136377-7">0-07-136377-7</a> – A physicist and an aeronautical engineer explain flight in non-technical terms and specifically address the equal-transit-time myth. They attribute airfoil circulation to the Coanda effect, which is controversial.</li>
<li><i>Aerodynamics</i>, Clancy, L. J. (1975), Section 4.8, Pitman Publishing Limited, London <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-273-01120-0" title="Special:BookSources/0-273-01120-0">0-273-01120-0</a>.</li>
<li><i>Aerodynamics, Aeronautics, and Flight Mechanics</i>, McCormick, Barnes W., (1979), Chapter 3, John Wiley &amp; Sons, Inc., New York <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-471-03032-5" title="Special:BookSources/0-471-03032-5">0-471-03032-5</a>.</li>
<li><i>Fundamentals of Flight</i>, Richard S. Shevell, Prentice-Hall International Editions, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r879151008" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-13-332917-8" title="Special:BookSources/0-13-332917-8">0-13-332917-8</a> – This is a text for a one-semester undergraduate course in mechanical or aeronautical engineering. Its sections on theory of flight are understandable with a passing knowledge of calculus and physics.</li>
<li>"Observation of Perfect Potential Flow in Superfluid", Paul P. Craig and John R. Pellam (1957) <i>Physical Review</i> <b>108</b>(5), pp. 1109–1112, <a href="/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" title="Digital object identifier">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1103%2FPhysRev.108.1109" rel="nofollow">10.1103/PhysRev.108.1109</a> – Experiments under <a href="/wiki/Superfluidity" title="Superfluidity">superfluidity</a> conditions, resulting in the vanishing of lift in inviscid flow since the <a href="/wiki/Kutta_condition" title="Kutta condition">Kutta condition</a> is no longer satisfied.</li>
<li>"Aerodynamics at the Particle Level", Charles A. Crummer (2005, revised 2012) – A treatment of aerodynamics emphasizing the particle nature of air, as opposed to the fluid approximation commonly used. <a class="external autonumber" href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/nlin/0507032.pdf" rel="nofollow">[8]</a></li>
<li>"Flight without Bernoulli" Chris Waltham Vol. 36, Nov. 1998 The Physics Teacher – using a physical model based on Newton’s second law, the author presents a rigorous fluid dynamical treatment of flight. <a class="external autonumber" href="http://www.df.uba.ar/users/sgil/physics_paper_doc/papers_phys/fluids/fly_no_bernoulli.pdf" rel="nofollow">[9]</a></li>
<li><i>Bernoulli, Newton, and Dynamic Lift</i> Norman F. Smith School Science and Mathematics vol 73 Part I: <a class="external autonumber" href="http://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/10.1111/j.1949-8594.1973.tb09040.x/pdf" rel="nofollow">[10]</a> Part II <a class="external autonumber" href="http://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/10.1111/j.1949-8594.1973.tb08998.x/pdf" rel="nofollow">[11]</a></li></ul>
</div>

<li><a class="external text" href="http://user.uni-frankfurt.de/~weltner/" rel="nofollow">Physics of Flight – reviewed. Online paper by Prof. Dr. Klaus Weltner</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.iop.org/EJ/article/0031-9120/38/6/001/pe3_6_001.pdf" rel="nofollow">How do Wings Work? – Holger Babinsky</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.planeandpilotmag.com/component/zine/article/289.html" rel="nofollow">Plane and Pilot Magazine Bernoulli Or Newton: Who's Right About Lift?</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=aFO4PBolwFg" rel="nofollow">One Minute Physics How Does a Wing actually work? (youtube video)</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20170422033534/https://www.zhaw.ch/de/forschung/personen-publikationen-projekte/detailansicht-publikation/publikation/212513/" rel="nofollow">From Summit to Seafloor - Lifted Weight as a Function of Altitude and Depth by Rolf Steinegger</a></li></ul>
